* [Fallanassi](/wiki/Fallanassi "Fallanassi")[[1]](#cite_note-Peace_and_Unity-1)
* [Force Priestesses](/wiki/Force_Priestesses "Force Priestesses")[[6]](#cite_note-Destiny-6)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:TitleOrPosition)

:   "*I can't use the Force. I don't feel it. Not like you do.*"  
    "*The Force resides in all living things. Even you.*"  
    "*If that's true, then why doesn't everyone use it?*"  
    "*Talent is a factor. But training and focus are what truly defines someone's success.* [...] *Not everyone can handle the type of discipline it takes to master the ways of the Force.*"
:   ―Sabine Wren and Ahsoka Tano[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17)

**Force-sensitives**, also known as **Force-users**, **Force wielders**, or **Force Adepts**, were [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") or non-sentient [lifeforms](/wiki/Species "Species") that possessed a strong connection to the mystical energy field known as [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). Awareness of [life energy](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force") and the capacity to tap into and guide its flow existed on a spectrum and was only possible due to the [symbiosis](/wiki/Symbiosis "Symbiosis") between individuals and [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian"), which communicated the will of the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force"). Individuals who focused and trained to attune with the Force could develop [abilities](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") that would otherwise be impossible.

Although the Force did not belong to any one group, usage of the Force for selfish and destructive purposes was categorized as the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), while dedicating to the will of the Force and the protection of life was deemed the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"). Force-sensitives could find the dark side to be easier to tap into as it was fueled by emotions, but the powers of that aspect of the Force were no greater than the discipline of the light and quickly corrupted its users, who were known as [dark side adepts](/wiki/Dark_side_adept "Dark side adept"). High levels of midi-chlorian allowed individuals to attune more readily to the Force, and individuals could inherit their [progenitors'](/wiki/Parent "Parent") power, as was the case in the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"). [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"), passed his gift to his children, the [twins](/wiki/Twin "Twin") [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), who, in turn, passed it to her son, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo").

Throughout [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history") various [religious](/wiki/Religion "Religion") orders have trained Force-sensitives to control their abilities, such as the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). During the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), Force-sensitives were hunted by a team of [Jedi hunters](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter") known as the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius"). A [Jedi holocron](/wiki/Jedi_holocron "Jedi holocron") containing a [Kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal "Kyber memory crystal") with a list of all known Force-sensitive [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") throughout [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") was [sought](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_rebuild_the_Jedi_Order "Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order") by the [Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister") and [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"). With the [destruction](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") of the Sith [Lords](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious and Darth Vader, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") Luke Skywalker [trained](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") a [generation](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") of Force-sensitive [students](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") in hopes of restoring the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"). His efforts were [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") until he and Leia Organa trained [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), who inherited Skywalker's mantle as the last Jedi after he [passed away](/wiki/Death "Death").

## Overview[]

### Terminology and basic information[]

:   "*I feel the Force.*"  
    "*But you cannot control it.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_V-18)

 [![Harnessing the power of the Force gave those sensitive to the spiritual energy extraordinary abilities.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428031515) [![Harnessing the power of the Force gave those sensitive to the spiritual energy extraordinary abilities.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190428031515)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428031515) 

Harnessing the power of the Force gave those sensitive to the spiritual energy extraordinary abilities.

 

[The Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") was a mysterious energy field that resided in all lifeforms,[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19) [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") and non-sentient alike,[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_V-18) binding [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") together[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19) along with the [universe](/wiki/Universe "Universe") as a whole.[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-20) While the Force resided in all living things, only some were strong enough to[[21]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-21) instinctively[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) feel its power.[[21]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-21) Former [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") compared natural Force-sensitivity to "talent."[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) They were classified as Force-sensitives,[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11) Force-users or Force Adepts.[[22]](#cite_note-Sly's_Card-22) These general terms applied to practitioners of the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"),[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) such as the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") and the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius"), although they were also referred to more specifically as "[dark side adepts](/wiki/Dark_side_adept "Dark side adept")."[[10]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_6-10)

Without training, knowledge or faith, a Force-sensitive's connection to the Force would remain dormant.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-24) The Force did not awaken within [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") until the nineteenth [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") in her life.[[13]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-13) Though untrained in its ways, Rey's Force ability was comparable to that of [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), formerly Ben Solo,[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-24) and their unique [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") allowed her to absorb some of his [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training"), giving Rey the ability to perform a few techniques such as [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") and [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick").[[21]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-21) Force-sensitives could be found in numerous [species](/wiki/Species "Species"), ranging from [humans](/wiki/Human "Human") and [humanoids](/wiki/Humanoid "Humanoid"), to various non-human [aliens](/wiki/Alien "Alien").[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_II-25) The few known members of [Yoda's species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species "Yoda's species") were Force-sensitive, including [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu"),[[26]](#cite_note-Chapter_2-26) Jedi Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle"), and Grand Master Yoda himself.[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27)

[Midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") indicated the strength of an individual's connection to the Force without any training to try and unlock it having occurred yet. They were microscopic organisms that resided in the [cells](/wiki/DNA "DNA") of all lifeforms and the more that a Force-sensitive was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") with, the stronger they could grow with the Force. [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") born of a [mother](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars") but no [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), had more midi-chlorians than any Force-sensitive of his [era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"), surpassing all [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and even Yoda at over twenty-thousand.[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27)

### To feel the Force[]

:   "*Why is Ben so much stronger? I work just as hard as he does.*"  
    "*Ben isn't stronger, Voe. That's not how it works. The Force can be a trickle, a stream, a river, a flood… for* anyone *who can sense it. Think of yourself as a door. The wider you open, the more easily the Force flows throughout you. Some people just start out with their door a bit more open. But any door can open wide.*"
:   ―Voe and Luke Skywalker[[28]](#cite_note-Kylo_3-28)

 [![Ezra Bridger and Darth Maul open the Holocrons to form a Holocron fusion showing themselves as Force-sensitives of the light side and dark side of the Force, respectively.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) [![Ezra Bridger and Darth Maul open the Holocrons to form a Holocron fusion showing themselves as Force-sensitives of the light side and dark side of the Force, respectively.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20161001154010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) 

Ezra Bridger and Darth Maul open the Holocrons to form a Holocron fusion showing themselves as Force-sensitives of the light side and dark side of the Force, respectively.

 

Although the Force did flow through all beings,[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) Force-sensitives, unlike regular beings, could harness[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) that flow[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) to access the power of the Force, giving them [extraordinary abilities](/wiki/Force_power "Force power").[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) Such was a natural application of the Force as it flowed through the sensitive; while the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") [cult](/wiki/Religion "Religion") claimed Force users like the Jedi "[enslaved](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery")" the Force to their will and used in the Force in unnatural ways,[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) earning Force-sensitives the names of "Force abusers" and "Force killers" amongst the cult,[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Char-Ryl-Roy](/wiki/Char-Ryl-Roy "Char-Ryl-Roy") rebuked their outlook. Instead, he remarked that the only unnatural thing in such a situation would be to try and deny one's connection to the Force and how it flowed through them, as it flowed through all lifeforms.[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) The degree to which one was Force-sensitive determined whether they were able to harness the Force's powers. [The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist") possessed a light sensitivity to the Force; as such, she could sense the Force but was not strong enough to use it.[[31]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-31) Those differing levels of Force-sensitivity existed even among those who could use the Force, with some beings more naturally sensitive than others: for example, the [sisters](/wiki/Zeveron_family "Zeveron family") [Elecia Zeveron](/wiki/Elecia_Zeveron "Elecia Zeveron") and [Oliviah Zeveron](/wiki/Oliviah_Zeveron "Oliviah Zeveron") were both Force users by birth, but Oliviah's connection to the Force was naturally stronger than that of her sister.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) While Elecia's connection to the Force remained mild into her adult life,[[32]](#cite_note-High_Republic_Character-32) she remained bitter towards the Jedi and believed she should have been taken instead of Oliviah.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30)

However, other individuals throughout [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history") demonstrated that, with time, someone without a great connection to the Force since birth could still rise in skill[[33]](#cite_note-What_a_Jedi_Makes-33) because the Force resided in them, as it did in all living beings.[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) [Lyr Farseeker](/wiki/Lyr_Farseeker "Lyr Farseeker") did not have a great deal of Force-sensitivity but would join the Jedi Order[[33]](#cite_note-What_a_Jedi_Makes-33) and arise to the rank of Jedi Master,[[34]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-34) writing some of the greatest texts of the Order during his life. When the boy [Lohim Nara](/wiki/Lohim_Nara "Lohim Nara") asked to join the Jedi Order but admitted he was not Force-sensitive, [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") urged the boy to read up on Farseeker and declared that the Force was not what made a Jedi, stating that only the boy himself could answer what made him a Jedi. While too old to beginning training as a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), Yoda offered the boy the position of guardian of the Temple.[[33]](#cite_note-What_a_Jedi_Makes-33) [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren") had less Force-sensitivity than any Padawan of the Jedi Order but was still trained by [Force-Sensitive Outcast](/wiki/Force-Sensitive_Outcast "Force-Sensitive Outcast") and former Jedi Ahsoka Tano, who believed Wren could connect to and harness the Force like her.[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17)

 [![Sabine Wren managed to unlock the power of the Force through training.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Sabine_pushes_Ezra_into_the_Chimaera.png/revision/latest?cb=20231006003857) [![Sabine Wren managed to unlock the power of the Force through training.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Sabine_pushes_Ezra_into_the_Chimaera.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20231006003857)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Sabine_pushes_Ezra_into_the_Chimaera.png/revision/latest?cb=20231006003857) 

Sabine Wren managed to unlock the power of the Force through training.

 

According to Tano, while the Force did reside in all living things, "talent" played a factor in terms of who was sensitive to it. Tano insisted that Wren could become attuned to the Force through training and focus. Wren had been quick to question why not everyone in the galaxy used the Force if everyone was connected to it, but Tano promised mastering the Force was a matter of discipline, with few in the galaxy maintaining that level of discipline.[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) Similarly, Luke Skywalker believed that one could not be "stronger" in the Force than another: when his apprentice [Voe](/wiki/Voe "Voe") grew upset at how natural the Force came to Skywalker's nephew [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), Luke told her that the Force was like a stream of water and herself a door in its path: the wider she opened herself to the Force, the easier it would be for the Force to flow through her. While some like Solo did start out their lives more sensitive, or their doors more open as he put it, Skywalker promised her she could open herself up, just as how any door could open wide.[[28]](#cite_note-Kylo_3-28)

Non-Force-sensitive members of the Path of the Open Hand once journeyed to [Planet X](/wiki/Sophros "Sophros"),[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) a living world[[35]](#cite_note-Eye_2-35) kept hidden by "[the Veil](/wiki/The_Veil_(Planet_X) "The Veil (Planet X)")"—which nearly destroyed their ship while trying to pass through it[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30)—in [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space").[[36]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-36) The Path agents were in pursuit of the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai"),[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) creatures who feasted upon the Living Force[[37]](#cite_note-Insider_221-37) and thus could be used as a weapon against the Jedi. While on planet, the individuals suddenly found themselves able to feel the energy of the Force as if they were sensitive to it. Two team members, [Shea Ganandra](/wiki/Shea_Ganandra "Shea Ganandra") and [Bokana Koss](/wiki/Bokana_Koss "Bokana Koss"), were even able to develop powers in the Force over their time on Planet X. However, an initial Force-sensitive of their team, [Calar](/wiki/Calar "Calar"), had begged them to stop the mission as they had passed through the Veil, having suddenly foreseen that their actions would have dire consequences that could "consume" the Force itself. The Veil was able to hone in on Force-sensitives as part of its efforts to hold back foreign bodies from landing on Planet X, with Calar trying to exploit that fact to destroy their expedition until he was killed by pilot [Radicaz Dobbs](/wiki/Radicaz_Dobbs "Radicaz Dobbs"). While on world, Koss had a similar vision to Calar's and warned of a "[blight](/wiki/Blight "Blight")," which he foretold would try to "chain" and kill the Force itself. Koss ultimately would die during the escape effort, but Ganandra did make it off Planet X and found her Force powers vanishing after leaving.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30)

In the case of the [Chiss](/wiki/Chiss "Chiss") species, however, there were instances of Force-sensitives losing their abilities despite receiving training and having the necessary discipline. [Chiss navigators](/wiki/Sky-walker "Sky-walker"), with a single [exception](/wiki/Vah%27nya "Vah'nya") universally lost their Force powers before adulthood regardless of training or practice.[[38]](#cite_note-Thrawn:_Alliances-38) Such was similar to how those born with a natural affinity for the Force could allow their powers to fade should they not be trained to fully harness them.[[39]](#cite_note-Chapter_13-39) Upon learning that the [Little](/wiki/Littles "Littles") [Utalir](/wiki/Utalir "Utalir") was Force-sensitive, something that even Utalir did not know and only came to light because she was targeted by a hungry Nameless, [Yana Ro](/wiki/Yana_Ro "Yana Ro") of the Path of the Open Hand pondered if her Force-sensitivity would develop in time or possibly remain dormant for as long as she lived.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) Alternatively, one sensitive to the Force could try and push it away to deny their own connection to the energy field. However, Jedi Padawan [Enya Keen](/wiki/Enya_Keen "Enya Keen") found that someone pushing away the Force was a different variation on using it, effectively two versions of the same theme; when she encountered the Force-sensitive [Binnot Ullo](/wiki/Binnot_Ullo "Binnot Ullo"), she sensed a disruption coming from the man and discovered it was his acts of pushing away the Force.[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) Finally, it was possible for someone—or, at least, someone well attuned to and skilled in the Force—to totally cut themself off from the Force as an act of [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)").[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-20)

 [![Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa were Force-sensitive by virtue of their lineage as the offspring of Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200613205339) [![Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa were Force-sensitive by virtue of their lineage as the offspring of Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200613205339)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke-Leia-training.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200613205339) 

Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa were Force-sensitive by virtue of their lineage as the offspring of Anakin Skywalker.

 

A Force-sensitive's offspring could be born with the same power,[[40]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-40) although, as Skywalker stated, that simply gave them an easier time connecting to the Force and anyone could rise to the same level with enough commitment.[[28]](#cite_note-Kylo_3-28) The [twins](/wiki/Twin "Twin") Luke Skywalker and [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") were second-generation Force-sensitives through their [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), Anakin Skywalker.[[40]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-40) Ben Solo was Organa's son and therefore a third-generation Force-sensitive in the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family").[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-20) Due to the potential of his bloodline, Solo was born with raw strength and the potential for limitless power.[[21]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-21) Apart from the Skywalkers, [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") inherited the power of her [paternal](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") [grandfather](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"), the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious").[[41]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-41)

## History[]

### Ancient origins[]

:   "*What is this place?*"  
    "*All that surround us is the foundation of life, the birthplace of what your science calls midi-chlorians, the foundation of what connects the Living Force and the Cosmic Force.*"
:   ―Yoda and Serenity[[6]](#cite_note-Destiny-6)

 [![The Ones were powerful beings who resided in the ethereal realm of Mortis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Force_Gods_of_Mortis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180120131819) [![The Ones were powerful beings who resided in the ethereal realm of Mortis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Force_Gods_of_Mortis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180120131819)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Force_Gods_of_Mortis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180120131819) 

The Ones were powerful beings who resided in the ethereal realm of Mortis.

 

The origins of the Force date back to a [mystical world](/wiki/Wellspring_of_Life "Wellspring of Life") believed to be the [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of the midi-chlorians. It was through the midi-chlorians that the energy of the [Living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force") fed into the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force"), which had a will of its own. In addition, the midi-chlorians existed in a symbiotic relationship with all lifeforms, particularly Force-sensitives who could harness the powers of the Force through the micro-organisms residing in their cells.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) A quintet of ancient entities, known as the [Force Priestesses](/wiki/Force_Priestesses "Force Priestesses"), dwelled on the unnamed world where the midi-chlorians were born. They embodied the link between the Living Force present in all lifeforms and the larger, timeless Cosmic Force.[[42]](#cite_note-Force_Priestesses_DB-42)

Though the Force existed throughout the universe, there were "[vergences](/wiki/Vergence "Vergence")" or nexus points of power that amplified the energy field and its effects. One such vergence was the legendary realm of [Mortis](/wiki/Mortis "Mortis"), home to [the Ones](/wiki/Force_wielder "Force wielder")—the [Daughter](/wiki/Daughter "Daughter"), who embodied the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"), the [Son](/wiki/Son "Son"), who embodied the dark side of the Force, and the [Father](/wiki/Father_(Mortis) "Father (Mortis)"), who represented the balance between them.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

### Fall of the Zeffo[]

:   "*It appears many, yet not all the Zeffo could wield the Force! They called it the "Life Wind" and those who wielded it, sages.*"
:   ―Eno Cordova[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

 [![Zeffo sages were Force-sensitive beings from a forgotten age that predated modern galactic civilization.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Eilram_sarcophagus_JFO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191205210537) [![Zeffo sages were Force-sensitive beings from a forgotten age that predated modern galactic civilization.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Eilram_sarcophagus_JFO.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191205210537)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Eilram_sarcophagus_JFO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191205210537) 

Zeffo sages were Force-sensitive beings from a forgotten age that predated modern galactic civilization.

 

Long before the time of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and Sith, the [ancient Zeffo civilization](/wiki/Zeffonian "Zeffonian") revered the Force or "Life Wind." While not every member of this race was strongly connected to the Force, the ones who were Force-sensitive became known as [sages](/wiki/Zeffo_Sage "Zeffo Sage"). The earliest Zeffo site was the [Tomb of Eilram](/wiki/Tomb_of_Eilram "Tomb of Eilram"); built on the [Zeffo](/wiki/Zeffo "Zeffo") homeworld, it was once a proving ground for Force-sensitive Zeffo, but was converted to honor their remains, Sage [Eilram](/wiki/Eilram "Eilram") in particular. Above all, it was built to honor the Life Wind. The same world was also the site of the [Tomb of Miktrull](/wiki/Tomb_of_Miktrull "Tomb of Miktrull"); Sage [Miktrull](/wiki/Miktrull "Miktrull") was a legendary Force wielder who was said to be all powerful. He was venerated as such and his tomb was more of a temple to his pride.[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

When the Zeffo began exploring the greater galaxy beyond their [home system](/wiki/Zeffo_system "Zeffo system"), they left behind monuments dedicated to the Life Wind on several worlds in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). [Bogano](/wiki/Bogano "Bogano") was one such planet; the Zeffo established their presence on this world by constructing [the Vault](/wiki/Bogano_Vault "Bogano Vault"), the interior of which was filled with pilgrims' offerings to the Life Wind. After the Zeffo established contact with the [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") of [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), they stored an [Astrium](/wiki/Astrium "Astrium")—a key that allowed Force-sensitives to perceive the mysteries of the vault on Bogano—at the pinnacle of the sacred [Origin Tree](/wiki/Origin_Tree "Origin Tree").[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

The Zeffo possessed knowledge of the dark side of the Force as well. Sage [Kujet](/wiki/Kujet "Kujet") was a ruthless [authoritarian](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") who harnessed the power of the dark side. The world of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir") became the site of his palace, the [Tomb of Kujet](/wiki/Tomb_of_Kujet "Tomb of Kujet"). Kujet's legacy was defined by his destruction of the Astriums and the lives of any who opposed his reign as sage. This included members of his own species, who rebelled against Kujet in hopes of ending his reign.[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

The Zeffo sages eventually foresaw the destruction of their civilization and the extinction of their species. They were convinced that their end was the result of their own creed, believing they had sacrificed balance for greater power and control. After the Zeffo fell to ultimate ruin, the history of their civilization was all but forgotten by the time of modern galactic civilization.[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

### Age of the Jedi[]

#### Wars of the Force[]

 [![Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice throughout the reign of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/HighRepublic-PhilNoto.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200226154428) [![Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice throughout the reign of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/HighRepublic-PhilNoto.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200226154428)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/HighRepublic-PhilNoto.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200226154428) 

Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice throughout the reign of the Galactic Republic.

 

In its heyday, the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") protected the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") as the guardians of peace and justice.[[43]](#cite_note-Jedi_Order_DB-43) Guided by the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code"), a philosophy centered on peace and calmness, and using the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") for knowledge and defense, the Jedi rejected the dark side and the emotions that channeled its power. As such, the Jedi emphasized the necessity for detachment and avoiding emotional attachments. It was the mission of the [Jedi seekers](/wiki/Jedi_seeker "Jedi seeker") to locate Force-sensitive infants and to bring them to the [Jedi temples](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple"), where they learned the ways of the Force alongside other [Jedi younglings](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate").[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

The Code was not embraced by all of the ancient Jedi, however. The Order was eventually divided by a [schism](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness") that led to the creation of the Sith—fallen Jedi who turned from the light, forming a dark-side cult that sought to unlock great powers and dominate those weaker than themselves. What began as a philosophical dispute gave way to open war between the Jedi and Sith, upending [galactic civilization](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and rendering entire [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") devoid of life. After millennia of conflict, the Jedi triumphed over the Sith and ushered the galaxy into a new age known as the [Great Peace](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"), becoming peacekeepers and negotiators for the Galactic Republic in lieu of a standing [military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military").[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

#### Era of the Light[]

:   "*You think using the Force is unnatural. We do not own the Force. We do not enslave it. It is the opposite. It flows through us. To deny the Force and how it moves through all beings—including the Jedi—that is unnatural.*"
:   ―Jedi Master Char-Ryl-Roy rebukes Path of the Open Hand member Goi Ganok[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29)

The Jedi identified Force-sensitive younglings and brought them to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27) The Jedi Order's efforts to recruit Force-sensitive [Bardottan](/wiki/Bardottan "Bardottan") children was opposed by another group of Force mystics, the [Dagoyan Order](/wiki/Dagoyan_Order "Dagoyan Order"), who saw the Jedi's actions as an affront to the sovereignty of their homeworld of [Bardotta](/wiki/Bardotta "Bardotta"). Though the Jedi returned the children to their families, the incident led to [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") of [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment").[[4]](#cite_note-NoP-4) Like their Jedi counterparts, the Dagoyan Masters possessed a strong connection to the Force, although their link to the energy field was more passive than that of the Jedi and Sith.[[44]](#cite_note-TDI-44) Rising to power in the Bardottan government, the Dagoyan Order became fully entrenched in their native culture and outlawed the [Frangawl Cult](/wiki/Frangawl_Cult "Frangawl Cult") for their devotion to the dark side of the Force.[[4]](#cite_note-NoP-4) The Jedi greatly expanded their activity throughout the galaxy during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"),[[45]](#cite_note-Kylo_2-45) during which time they partnered with other Force religions on the moon of Jedha.[[46]](#cite_note-Convergence-46)

 [![The Jedi Order and various other Force religions partnered on Jedha, only to face conflict from the Path of the Open Hand cult.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/ConvocationChambers-2022THR4.png/revision/latest?cb=20231104112652) [![The Jedi Order and various other Force religions partnered on Jedha, only to face conflict from the Path of the Open Hand cult.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/ConvocationChambers-2022THR4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231104112652)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/ConvocationChambers-2022THR4.png/revision/latest?cb=20231104112652) 

The Jedi Order and various other Force religions partnered on Jedha, only to face conflict from the Path of the Open Hand cult.

 

Beyond working with groups like the [Sorcerers of Tund](/wiki/Sorcerers_of_Tund "Sorcerers of Tund") and [Church of the Force](/wiki/Church_of_the_Force "Church of the Force") as part of Jedha's governing [convocation](/wiki/Convocation_of_the_Force "Convocation of the Force"),[[1]](#cite_note-Peace_and_Unity-1) ensuring a diverse grouping of perspectives could gather to discuss the Force,[[36]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-36) the Jedi brought orphaned children who were too old to start Jedi training to Jedha, where they could be adopted by other orders.[[46]](#cite_note-Convergence-46) Dark side groups were not invited to join the Convocation of the Force.[[1]](#cite_note-Peace_and_Unity-1) During the Republic's expansion amid the High Republic Era, however, the Jedi would cross paths with the Path of the Open Hand cult, which wrongly preached that the Force needed to be "freed" from use, on the planet [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna"). Force-sensitives were allowed to join the Path, but they were made to suppress their natural connection to the Force in the name of the Path's beliefs. Under the influence of its leader, Elecia Zeveron, the Path launched a campaign to wipe out Force users with members of the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai") species,[[36]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-36) kicking off the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha") and bringing chaos to the Holy Moon.[[47]](#cite_note-Battle_of_Jedha-47)

The Battle of Jedha had its roots in religious tensions between the various faiths who called Jedha holy, but, after the battle, the peoples of Jedha then rallied together to rebuild their home.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) Another member of the Path was a Force-sensitive [Mirialan](/wiki/Mirialan "Mirialan") named [Binnot Ullo](/wiki/Binnot_Ullo "Binnot Ullo"), who rejected and pushed away his own Force-sensitivity as per the Path's ideals. However, Jedi Knight [Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai") deduced that he was someone who used the Force whenever it suited him, something the Path would punish him for if it were widely known, although he tried to deny her accusation. Ullo and fellow Path member [Goi Ganok](/wiki/Goi_Ganok "Goi Ganok") were involved in an undercover mission after the Battle of Jedha to ensure the [Eiram and E'ronoh War](/wiki/Eiram_and_E%27ronoh_War "Eiram and E'ronoh War") would continue, during which time Ganok accidentally revealed their true loyalties, in part by calling Force healing an unnatural ability. Jedi Master Char-Ryl-Roy would rebuke Ganok and the overall Path ideology during their confrontation, remarking that the true unnatural ideal in the situation was that the Path rejected how the Force actually operated to fit its beliefs.[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29)

In the end, the Path's conflict with the Jedi would end with the so-called [Night of Sorrow](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), a battle waged by the Path on its homeworld of [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna"). The Jedi, the Republic, and the allied peoples of [Eiram](/wiki/Eiram "Eiram") and [E'ronoh](/wiki/E%27ronoh "E'ronoh") put down the Path after many losses were sustained, in part by the release of Nameless onto the battlefield by the Path. Ullo himself would be killed at the battle's close,[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) as would Zeveron, whom [Path Guide](/wiki/Guide_of_the_Closed_Fist "Guide of the Closed Fist") [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro") learned was actually a Force-sensitive who hated the Jedi Order because it did not take her in. While even she had been horrified by the effects of the Nameless, Marda retained control over the Leveler and used it to kill Zeveron in the first act of her new plan to "free" the Force.[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) After the battle, Jedi Masters Yoda and [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun") decided to cover up the existence of the Nameless until more information on the threat they posed could be uncovered,[[29]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-29) but Ro escaped with knowledge of the creatures[[30]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-30) that would be passed down to subsequent generations of her family, the [Ro's](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family").[[48]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-48)

#### Rise of the Dark[]

:   "*The Force is unusually strong with him. That much is clear.*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn, on Anakin Skywalker[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27)

 [![Anakin Skywalker was a Force-sensitive life form whose blood contained the highest known midi-chlorian count.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/AnakinSkywalkerEpIII-SWFB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200823195028) [![Anakin Skywalker was a Force-sensitive life form whose blood contained the highest known midi-chlorian count.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/AnakinSkywalkerEpIII-SWFB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200823195028)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/AnakinSkywalkerEpIII-SWFB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200823195028) 

Anakin Skywalker was a Force-sensitive life form whose blood contained the highest known midi-chlorian count.

 

Rising to power in the [last remaining years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the Republic, a Force-sensitive politician rose to power in the ranks of the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"). His connection to the Force a closely guarded secret, Sheev Palpatine was elected to the office of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor")[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) as a result of the crisis on his homeworld, the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo").[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27) Also unbeknownst to his colleagues, the former [senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") from [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") was in fact the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"), [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, heir to the [reformed Sith](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two") founded by [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane"). As Sidious plotted the Sith's return to power,[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) Anakin Skywalker was discovered by Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn"). Intrigued by the child's raw power with the Force, Jinn found that Skywalker had a higher concentration of midi-chlorians in his cells than any other lifeforms, including Grand Master Yoda. In addition, the information that Skywalker was conceived without a father led Jinn to suspect that this Force-sensitive boy was created through the midi-chlorians. Jinn ultimately brought Skywalker to the Jedi Temple, having concluded that the young [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") from [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") was the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") of Jedi prophecy,[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27) destined to bring balance to the Force by destroying the Sith.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

The Jedi Order kept records of all known Force-sensitive infants that had yet to be taken to the Temple for training.[[49]](#cite_note-HH-49) During the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), several infants were abducted and brought to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") on the orders of Darth Sidious, who foresaw an army of dark side adepts serving as extensions of his will. Before they could be subjected to experimentation, the children were rescued by Skywalker, who had risen to the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), and his [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano").[[50]](#cite_note-Children-50)

By the end of the conflict, the Jedi were vanquished through Sidious' machinations to take over the Republic, installing himself on a [throne](/wiki/Throne "Throne") as [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). He had also lured Skywalker to the dark side of the Force, transforming the Jedi Order's Chosen One into a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") called Darth Vader. The newly anointed Sith Lord [marched on the Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") to kill his former brothers in the Force, including the Force-sensitive younglings who represented the future of the Order.[[51]](#cite_note-Episode_III-51)

### Reign of the Galactic Empire[]

:   "*What empire?"  
    "THE Empire. The one bent on exterminating Force-sensitives so no one can stand against it?*"
:   ―Merrin and Cal Kestis[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

 [![With the Jedi Order's destruction, the Sith rose to power as the secret rulers of the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208034628) [![With the Jedi Order's destruction, the Sith rose to power as the secret rulers of the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130208034628)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208034628) 

With the Jedi Order's destruction, the Sith rose to power as the secret rulers of the Galactic Empire.

 

Though its founder, [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), was secretly Force-sensitive, the newly formed [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") went to great lengths suppressing the memory of the Jedi and knowledge of the Force. Imperial [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") had spread disinformation about the fallen Order, claiming the Jedi were charlatans and the Force a primitive superstition. While the Empire consolidated its rule over the galaxy, the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius")—[Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") survivors who turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force")—hunted both Jedi and other Force-sensitives, including children.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

 [![Force-sensitives were persecuted during the Imperial Era, with even children being targeted by the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/VaderInquisitorsKothsDaughter-2017DarthVader19.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112052212) [![Force-sensitives were persecuted during the Imperial Era, with even children being targeted by the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/VaderInquisitorsKothsDaughter-2017DarthVader19.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240112052212)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/VaderInquisitorsKothsDaughter-2017DarthVader19.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112052212) 

Force-sensitives were persecuted during the Imperial Era, with even children being targeted by the Empire.

 

The few remaining Jedi were determined to rebuild the Order; during the early years of the Empire's reign, former Padawan [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr") began training one of his [disciples](/wiki/Ferren_Barr%27s_disciples "Ferren Barr's disciples"), the Force-sensitive [Verla](/wiki/Verla "Verla"), in the Jedi arts. Although he was unable to complete Verla's training before his [demise](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala") at the hands of Darth Vader on [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala"), Barr instructed his apprentice to seek out other survivors, believing the Order would eventually return through a new generation of Jedi that included Verla.[[52]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-52)

The former Jedi [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda") had the same idea; the Order's resurrection was dependent on the training of new apprentices. After rescuing Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis") on [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"), the two Jedi fugitives embarked on a [secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_rebuild_the_Jedi_Order "Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order"). To complete this objective, they sought a [holocron](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") that once belonged to Junda's master, [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova"). This holocron contained a list of all known Force-sensitive infants in the galaxy, given to Cordova by [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu") as a fail-safe in the event of the Order's prophesied destruction. Though Kestis eventually retrieved the holocron, overcoming various obstacles in his path, including Junda's fallen apprentice, the Inquisitor once known as [Trilla Suduri](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"), he had foreseen that his efforts to rebuild the Order would end in the abduction and [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") of his acolytes. After surviving a confrontation with Darth Vader, Kestis chose to keep the children's identities secret by destroying the holocron, leaving their fate in the hands of the Force.[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11)

 [![The Jedi tradition was preserved by a handful of survivors despite the Empire's efforts to eradicate the last traces of their order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/CereKnightsCal.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223174926) [![The Jedi tradition was preserved by a handful of survivors despite the Empire's efforts to eradicate the last traces of their order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/CereKnightsCal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200223174926)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/CereKnightsCal.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223174926) 

The Jedi tradition was preserved by a handful of survivors despite the Empire's efforts to eradicate the last traces of their order.

 

Though Kestis and Junda abandoned their plan to train a new generation of Jedi,[[11]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-11) another Jedi fugitive, [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), took an apprentice of his own despite his incomplete training. While operating as an [anti-Imperial insurgent](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") on [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), the Jedi-turned-rebel encountered [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), a young orphan and small-time thief who possessed a strong connection to the Force. Though Bridger agreed to learn the ways of the Force from Jarrus, their partnership proved difficult for a master who never finished his own training and a headstrong apprentice with authority issues. However, as time passed the two were able to work more effectively, allowing Bridger to hone his Force abilities and use his power more responsibly with Jarrus' guidance.[[53]](#cite_note-Ezra_DB-53)

 [![As a Force-sensitive Luke Skywalker sought to become a Jedi Knight, like his father before him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LukeSkywalker-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407043449) [![As a Force-sensitive Luke Skywalker sought to become a Jedi Knight, like his father before him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LukeSkywalker-TLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230407043449)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LukeSkywalker-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407043449) 

As a Force-sensitive Luke Skywalker sought to become a Jedi Knight, like his father before him.

 

Unbeknownst to Vader, [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), the late wife of his former self, gave birth to the twin siblings Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa. They were both strong in the Force, having inherited their father's Force ability. In order to protect them from the Sith, Jedi Masters [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and Yoda had the twins separated, with Skywalker sent to his [relatives](/wiki/Lars_family "Lars family") on Tatooine while his sister was raised as a [princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") by the [royal house](/wiki/House_of_Organa "House of Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"). Though barely trained by the time of the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), Skywalker showed immense potential. With the Force guiding his actions, he destroyed the planet-killing [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon"), the [DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), shaking the Empire's rule to its foundations and bringing a newfound sense of hope to the fledgling Rebellion.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

The Sith Lords endeavored to turn Skywalker to the dark side of the Force, knowing that he could destroy everything they had built if he completed his training as a Jedi. Vader sought to succeed his master by becoming Emperor with his son at his side, while Sidious saw an opportunity to gain a younger and stronger apprentice. Their efforts culminated in a final showdown between father and son during the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), where Skywalker triumphed but refused to strike Vader down. Luke's defiance toward the Emperor awakened Vader's former self, Anakin Skywalker, who cast his dark master down a [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") shaft in order to save his son. In doing so, he killed the Emperor at the cost of his own life, yet by destroying the Sith he also fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

### A new generation[]

:   "*For many years, there was balance, and then I saw… Ben. My nephew with that mighty Skywalker blood. And in my hubris, I thought I could train him; I could pass on my strengths. Han was…Han about it, but… Leia trusted me with her son. I took him, and a dozen students, and began a training temple.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-20)

 [![Skywalker trained a new generation of Force-sensitive students, which included his powerful nephew, Ben Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) [![Skywalker trained a new generation of Force-sensitive students, which included his powerful nephew, Ben Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250306232725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) 

Skywalker trained a new generation of Force-sensitive students, which included his powerful nephew, Ben Solo.

 

With the Sith vanquished, the [Empire shattered](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") and the Force in balance, Luke Skywalker spent years pondering his next move, unsure about whether to rebuild the Jedi Order. The Force offered no guidance on this matter, and so Skywalker traveled across the galaxy searching for answers as a Jedi and for himself. His decision to ultimately pass on his knowledge was due to the most personal of reasons—his nephew Ben Solo. Skywalker recognized that his sister's son was extraordinarily strong with the Force, but also in desperate need of a teacher due to his volatile nature.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23)

However, the Jedi Order [fell back into ruin](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") after Solo fell to the dark side, like his grandfather before him. Adopting the identity of Kylo Ren, the former Jedi became the apprentice of [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") while Skywalker withdrew into exile on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"), determined to see the Jedi tradition end with his eventual death as the last Jedi. But the will of the Force, which had remained dormant ever since Anakin restored the balance, awakened once more when a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") from [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), named Rey, discovered her latent abilities as a Force-sensitive.[[23]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-23) Unbeknownst to both herself and Ren, they were a [dyad in the Force](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad")—two beings who shared a unique Force-bond uniting them across time and space.[[13]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-13)

| [Wiki-shrinkable](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Wiki-shrinkable.png/revision/latest?cb=20060123022626) This article is a [stub](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Stub "Wookieepedia:Stub"). You can help Wookieepedia by [expanding it](/wiki/Special:EditPage/Force-sensitive "Special:EditPage/Force-sensitive"). |
| --- |

## Behind the scenes[]

:   "*I suspect the term "Force-sensitive" (which dates back to 1978's Splinter of the Mind's Eye, btw) may confuse things. If it's at all helpful, think of "gifted" or "talented" as an analog.*"
:   ―Pablo Hidalgo[[54]](#cite_note-Pablo_Twitter_1-54)

The term "Force-sensitive" was first used in the [1978](/wiki/1978 "1978") [Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") novel *[Splinter of the Mind's Eye](/wiki/Splinter_of_the_Mind%27s_Eye "Splinter of the Mind's Eye")*.[[54]](#cite_note-Pablo_Twitter_1-54) Following the release of *[Star Wars: Ahsoka](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Ahsoka "Star Wars: Ahsoka")* "[Part Three: Time to Fly](/wiki/Part_Three:_Time_to_Fly "Part Three: Time to Fly")," which discussed the idea that Sabine Wren could learn to sense the Force,[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* Lore Adviser [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo") advised fans to think of "Force-sensitive" as a term akin to "gifted" or "talented,"[[54]](#cite_note-Pablo_Twitter_1-54) the latter term Tano had used in the episode itself.[[17]](#cite_note-Part_Three-17) Indeed, [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") stated in *[The Making of Return of the Jedi](/wiki/The_Making_of_Return_of_the_Jedi "The Making of Return of the Jedi")* that everyone had the potential to use the Force, but only the Jedi took the time to train,[[55]](#cite_note-Making-55) with later works depicting Force orders, like the Sith, that also took the time to train their members.[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_I-27)[[15]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-15)[[8]](#cite_note-TD1-8) In the [interview](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Archives:_Episodes_I%E2%80%93III,_1999%E2%80%932005 "The Star Wars Archives: Episodes I–III, 1999–2005") given to [Paul Duncan](/wiki/Paul_Duncan "Paul Duncan"), author of the *[Star Wars Archives](/wiki/Star_Wars_Archives "Star Wars Archives")* books, Lucas retracted that statement saying only those with enough Midi-chlorians in their body could "have a certain amount of control over our Personal Force and learn how to use it, like the Buddhist practice of being able to walk on hot coals."[[56]](#cite_note-The_Star_Wars_Archives:_Episodes_I–III,_1999–2005-56)

Hidalgo compared Force-sensitivity to someone with an "ear for music" because whatever natural talent one has still needs to be practiced.[[57]](#cite_note-Pablo_Twitter_2-57) Hidalgo did admit the presence of Midi-chlorians complicated the analogy, but he stated midi-chlorians are no real promise of someone's skill and that everyone in the galaxy has them.[[58]](#cite_note-Pablo_Twitter_3-58)

An [unfinished Clone Wars episode](/wiki/The_Clone_Wars_Legacy "The Clone Wars Legacy") had young Ahsoka Tano being kidnapped by a [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") named [Latrans](/wiki/Unidentified_false_Jedi "Unidentified false Jedi"). [Dave Filoni](/wiki/Dave_Filoni "Dave Filoni") presumed that, due to the rarity of Force-sensitives in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), they were highly sought after and some may have attempted to kidnap them.[[59]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_Panel_Video-59)
